# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 02:23:19.714255

### Base Program

```py
def maximum69Number(num: int) -> int:
    num_str = list(str(num))
    for i in range(len(num_str)):
        if num_str[i] == '6':
            num_str[i] = '9'
            break
    return int(''.join(num_str))
```

### Input

```json
[81]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def maximum69Number(num: int) -> int:
    num_str = list(str(num))
    for i in range(len(num_str)):
        if num_str[i] == '6':
            num_str[i] = '9'
            break
    return int(''.join(num_str))
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def maximum69Number(var_0: int) -> int:
    num_str = list(str(var_0))
    for i in range(len(num_str)):
        if num_str[i] == '6':
            num_str[i] = '9'
            break
    return int(''.join(num_str))
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def maximum69Number(var_1: int) -> int:
    num_str = list(str(var_1))
    for i in range(len(num_str)):
        if num_str[i] == '6':
            num_str[i] = '9'
            break
    return int(''.join(num_str))
```
